\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_node__modules_2rollup_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md24240}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{2.\+0.\+0}{2.0.0}}\label{md_node__modules_2rollup_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md24240}
{\itshape 2020-\/03-\/06}\hypertarget{md_node__modules_2rollup_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md24241}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Breaking Changes}{Breaking Changes}}\label{md_node__modules_2rollup_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md24241}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Rollup now requires at least Node 10 to run, or a sufficiently modern browser (\#3346)
\item The file structure of Rollup\textquotesingle{}s ESM builds has changed\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The main ESM entry point is now at {\ttfamily rollup/dist/es/rollup.\+js} instead of {\ttfamily rollup/dist/rollup.\+es.\+js}
\item The ESM browser build is at {\ttfamily rollup/dist/es/rollup.\+browser.\+js} instead of {\ttfamily rollup/dist/rollup.\+browser.\+es.\+js}
\end{DoxyItemize}

In general, the ESM builds now follow the same naming scheme as the CJS builds but are located in the {\ttfamily rollup/dist/es} subfolder instead of {\ttfamily rollup/dist} (\#3391)
\item The "{}watch.\+chokidar"{} option no longer accepts a {\ttfamily boolean} value but only an object of parameters that is passed to the bundled Chokidar instance. Chokidar installations by the user will be ignored in favour of the bundled instance (\#3331)
\item Modules that are completely tree-\/shaken will no longer be listed as part of any chunks in {\ttfamily generate\+Bundle}
\item The {\ttfamily experimental\+Optimize\+Chunks} and {\ttfamily chunk\+Grouping\+Size} options have been removed
\item \href{https://github.com/acornjs/acorn}{\texttt{ acorn}} plugins can only be used if they accept a passed-\/in acorn instance instead of importing it themselves. See \href{https://github.com/acornjs/acorn/pull/870\#issuecomment-527339830}{\texttt{ https\+://github.\+com/acornjs/acorn/pull/870\#issuecomment-\/527339830}} for what needs to be done to make plugins compatible that do not support this yet (\#3391)
\item Emitted chunks now have the Type\+Script type {\ttfamily Uint8\+Array} instead of {\ttfamily Buffer}. A {\ttfamily Buffer} can still be used, though (\#3395)
\item The Type\+Script types no longer use ESTree types for AST nodes but a very generic type that does not contain information specific to certain node types (\#3395)
\item The signature of the {\ttfamily write\+Bundle} plugin hook has been changed to match {\ttfamily generate\+Bundle}\+: The bundle object is now passed as second parameter instead of first and the first parameter is the output options (\#3361)
\item The following plugin hooks have been removed\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item ongenerate\+: use {\ttfamily generate\+Bundle} instead
\item onwrite\+: use {\ttfamily write\+Bundle} instead
\item transform\+Bundle\+: use {\ttfamily render\+Chunk} instead
\item transform\+Chunk\+: use {\ttfamily render\+Chunk} instead
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item You can no longer access {\ttfamily this.\+watcher} on the plugin context.
\item The {\ttfamily transform} hook can no longer return {\ttfamily dependencies}.
\item The {\ttfamily treeshake.\+pure\+External\+Modules} option will now show a deprecation warning when used\+: use `treeshake.\+module\+Side\+Effects\+: \textquotesingle{}no-\/external'{\ttfamily instead}
\item {\ttfamily Using}import.\+meta.\+ROLLUP\+\_\+\+ASSET\+\_\+\+URL\+\_\+$<$..$>${\ttfamily and}import.\+meta.\+ROLLUP\+\_\+\+CHUNK\+\_\+\+URL\+\_\+$<$..$>${\ttfamily in code will now show warnings\+: use}import.\+meta.\+ROLLUP\+\_\+\+FILE\+\_\+\+URL\+\_\+$<$..$>${\ttfamily instead}
\item {\ttfamily The}resolve\+Asset\+Url{\ttfamily hook will now show a deprecation warning when used\+: use}resolve\+File\+Url{\ttfamily instead}
\item {\ttfamily The following plugin context functions will show warnings when used\+: -\/}this.\+emit\+Asset{\ttfamily \+: use}this.\+emit\+File{\ttfamily  -\/}this.\+emit\+Chunk{\ttfamily \+: use}this.\+emit\+File{\ttfamily  -\/}this.\+get\+Asset\+File\+Name{\ttfamily \+: use}this.\+get\+File\+Name{\ttfamily  -\/}this.\+get\+Chunk\+File\+Name{\ttfamily \+: use}this.\+get\+File\+Name{\ttfamily  -\/}this.\+is\+External{\ttfamily \+: use}this.\+resolve{\ttfamily  -\/}this.\+resolve\+Id{\ttfamily \+: use}this.\+resolve{\ttfamily }
\item {\ttfamily Directly adding properties to the bundle object in the}generate\+Bundle{\ttfamily is deprecated will show a warning (removing properties is allowed, though)\+: Use}this.\+emit\+File{\ttfamily }
\item {\ttfamily Accessing}chunk.\+is\+Asset{\ttfamily on the bundle is deprecated\+: Use}chunk.\+type === \textquotesingle{}asset\textquotesingle{}{\ttfamily instead}
\item {\ttfamily The error code for a missing}name{\ttfamily property when targeting UMD has been changed to}MISSING\+\_\+\+NAME\+\_\+\+OPTION\+\_\+\+FOR\+\_\+\+IIFE\+\_\+\+EXPORT\`{} to emphasize this is needed for the IIFE part of UMD (\#3393)
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_node__modules_2rollup_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md24242}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Features}{Features}}\label{md_node__modules_2rollup_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md24242}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Rollup now bundles \href{https://github.com/paulmillr/chokidar}{\texttt{ Chokidar}} for a better watch experience (\#3331)
\item Rollup now bundles \href{https://github.com/acornjs/acorn}{\texttt{ acorn}} again, removing its only external dependency (\#3391)
\item Do not consider empty imports from side-\/effect-\/free modules for chunking and hoist side-\/effect imports if necessary (\#3369)
\item Rollup can now be imported as an ES module in Node via `import \{rollup\} from \textquotesingle{}rollup'{\ttfamily . Note that this relies on Node\textquotesingle{}s experimental \mbox{[}conditional package exports\mbox{]}(\href{https://nodejs.org/dist/latest-v13.x/docs/api/esm.html}{\texttt{ https\+://nodejs.\+org/dist/latest-\/v13.\+x/docs/api/esm.\+html}}\#esm\+\_\+conditional\+\_\+exports) feature and is therefore itself experimental (\#3391) -\/}systemjs{\ttfamily can be used as format alias for}system\`{} (\#3381)
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_node__modules_2rollup_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md24243}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Bug Fixes}{Bug Fixes}}\label{md_node__modules_2rollup_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md24243}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Unknown output options now trigger a warning when using the Java\+Script API (\#3352)
\item Rollup will no longer introduce Node types into Type\+Script projects that do not use them (\#3395)
\item Generate correct sourcemaps when tree-\/shaking occurs in a multi-\/file bundle (\#3423)
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_node__modules_2rollup_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md24244}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Pull Requests}{Pull Requests}}\label{md_node__modules_2rollup_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md24244}

{\itshape 2019-\/01-\/03}\hypertarget{md_node__modules_2rollup_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md24618}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Bug Fixes}{Bug Fixes}}\label{md_node__modules_2rollup_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md24618}

\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_node__modules_2rollup_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md24620}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{1.\+0.\+0}{1.0.0}}\label{md_node__modules_2rollup_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md24620}
{\itshape 2018-\/12-\/28}\hypertarget{md_node__modules_2rollup_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md24621}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Breaking Changes}{Breaking Changes}}\label{md_node__modules_2rollup_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md24621}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Several (mostly deprecated) options have been removed or renamed (\#2293, \#2409)\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item banner -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} output.\+banner
\item dest -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} output.\+file
\item entry -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} input
\item experimental\+Code\+Splitting -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} now always active
\item experimental\+Dynamic\+Import -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} now always active
\item experimental\+Preserve\+Modules -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} preserve\+Modules
\item exports -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} output.\+exports
\item extend -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} output.\+extend
\item footer -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} output.\+footer
\item format -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} output.\+format
\item freeze -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} output.\+freeze
\item globals -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} output.\+globals
\item indent -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} output.\+indent
\item interop -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} output.\+interop
\item intro -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} output.\+intro
\item load -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} use plugin API
\item module\+Name -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} output.\+name
\item name -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} output.\+name
\item no\+Conflict -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} output.\+no\+Conflict
\item output.\+module\+Id -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} output.\+amd.\+id
\item outro -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} output.\+outro
\item paths -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} output.\+paths
\item prefer\+Const -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} output.\+prefer\+Const
\item pure\+External\+Modules -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} treeshake.\+pure\+External\+Modules
\item resolve\+External -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} use plugin API
\item resolve\+Id -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} use plugin API
\item sourcemap -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} output.\+sourcemap
\item source\+Map -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} output.\+sourcemap
\item source\+Map\+File -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} output.\+sourcemap\+File
\item strict -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} output.\+strict
\item targets -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} use output as an array
\item transform -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} use plugin API
\item use\+Strict -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} output.\+strict
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item In general, output options can no longer be used as input options (\#2409)
\item {\ttfamily bundle.\+generate} and {\ttfamily bundle.\+write} now return a new format (\#2293)
\item Several plugin hooks have become deprecated and will display warnings when used (\#2409)\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item transform\+Bundle
\item transform\+Chunk
\item ongenerate
\item onwrite
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Plugin transform dependencies are deprecated in favour of using the {\ttfamily this.\+add\+Watch\+File} plugin context function (\#2409)
\item Accessing {\ttfamily this.\+watcher} in plugin hooks is deprecated in favour of the {\ttfamily watch\+Change} plugin hook and the {\ttfamily this.\+add\+Watch\+File} plugin context function (\#2409)
\item Using dynamic import statements will by default create a new chunk unless {\ttfamily inline\+Dynamic\+Imports} is used (\#2293)
\item Rollup now uses acorn@6 which means that acorn plugins must be compatible with this version; acorn is now external for non-\/browser builds to make plugins work (\#2293)
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_node__modules_2rollup_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md24622}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Features}{Features}}\label{md_node__modules_2rollup_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md24622}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The {\ttfamily -\/-\/dir} ClI option can now be aliased as {\ttfamily -\/d} (\#2293)
\item The {\ttfamily -\/-\/input} option now supports named entry points via {\ttfamily =} (\#2293)
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_node__modules_2rollup_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md24623}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Bug Fixes}{Bug Fixes}}\label{md_node__modules_2rollup_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md24623}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Both the {\ttfamily -\/-\/input} option as well as the default CLI option now support named inputs (\#2293)
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_node__modules_2rollup_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md24624}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Pull Requests}{Pull Requests}}\label{md_node__modules_2rollup_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md24624}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \href{https://github.com/rollup/rollup/pull/2293}{\texttt{ \#2293}}\+: Unify code paths for 1.\+0 relase and update documentation (@guybedford and @lukastaegert)
\item \href{https://github.com/rollup/rollup/pull/2409}{\texttt{ \#2409}}\+: Remove old deprecated features and add new deprecation warnings (@guybedford)
\item \href{https://github.com/rollup/rollup/pull/2486}{\texttt{ \#2486}}\+: Upgrade to acorn 6 (@marijnh)
\item \href{https://github.com/rollup/rollup/pull/2611}{\texttt{ \#2611}}\+: Fix hook\textquotesingle{}s name in test description (@\+Andarist)
\item \href{https://github.com/rollup/rollup/pull/2612}{\texttt{ \#2612}}\+: Fix a self-\/contradicting comment in the docs (@\+Long\+Teng\+Dao)
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_node__modules_2rollup_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md24625}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{0.\+68.\+2}{0.68.2}}\label{md_node__modules_2rollup_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md24625}
{\itshape 2018-\/12-\/23}\hypertarget{md_node__modules_2rollup_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md24626}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Bug Fixes}{Bug Fixes}}\label{md_node__modules_2rollup_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md24626}

\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_node__modules_2rollup_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md24627}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Pull Requests}{Pull Requests}}\label{md_node__modules_2rollup_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md24627}

{\itshape 2018-\/12-\/19}\hypertarget{md_node__modules_2rollup_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md24629}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Bug Fixes}{Bug Fixes}}\label{md_node__modules_2rollup_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md24629}

\begin{DoxyItemize}

\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_node__modules_2rollup_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md24630}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Pull Requests}{Pull Requests}}\label{md_node__modules_2rollup_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md24630}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \href{https://github.com/rollup/rollup/pull/2600}{\texttt{ \#2600}}\+: Fix UMD and IIFE wrapper issues and add comprehensive functional wrapper tests (@lukastaegert)
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_node__modules_2rollup_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md24631}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{0.\+68.\+0}{0.68.0}}\label{md_node__modules_2rollup_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md24631}
{\itshape 2018-\/12-\/16}\hypertarget{md_node__modules_2rollup_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md24632}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Breaking Changes}{Breaking Changes}}\label{md_node__modules_2rollup_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md24632}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily optimize\+Chunks} is renamed to {\ttfamily experimental\+Optimize\+Chunks} to reflect this feature is not production-\/ready yet (\#2575)
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_node__modules_2rollup_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md24633}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Features}{Features}}\label{md_node__modules_2rollup_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md24633}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Plugins can iterate all module ids via {\ttfamily this.\+module\+Ids} (\#2565)
\item Plugins can get graph information about a module via {\ttfamily this.\+get\+Module\+Info(id)} (\#2565)
\item Plugins and JS API users get more information about the generated chunks\+: {\ttfamily dynamic\+Imports}, {\ttfamily facade\+Module\+Id}, {\ttfamily is\+Dynamic\+Entry}, {\ttfamily name} (\#2575)
\item Tree-\/shaken dynamic imports will no longer create chunks or influence chunking in any way (\#2575)
\item Dynamic imports will no longer follow the {\ttfamily entry\+File\+Names} but the {\ttfamily chunk\+File\+Names} property reflecting those are solely internally used (\#2575)
\item If there are chunk naming conflicts, entry chunks will always take precedence (\#2575)
\item If an entry facade is created, only the facade chunk is marked as {\ttfamily is\+Entry} (\#2575)
\item Dynamic chunks will only be marked as {\ttfamily is\+Entry} if they are actually entry chunks as well; thus there is now a 1-\/to-\/1 correspondence between modules listed in {\ttfamily input} and chunks marked as {\ttfamily is\+Entry} (\#2575)
\item Chunks no longer contain imports for variables that are tree-\/shaken in the chunk but used in other chunks (\#2584)
\item Chunks will always import re-\/exported variables directly from the chunk where they are originally exported from (\#2584)
\item Null characters will be pruned from chunk ids to allow for virtually created chunks and make {\ttfamily rollup-\/plugin-\/multi-\/entry} compatible with code-\/splitting and thus the upcoming 1.\+0 version (\#2590)
\item Simplify the UMD wrapper code as much as possible, especially if there are no exports (\#2594)
\item The UMD wrapper will now work in strict mode by checking for {\ttfamily self} before {\ttfamily this} when determining the global variable (\#2594)
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_node__modules_2rollup_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md24634}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Bug Fixes}{Bug Fixes}}\label{md_node__modules_2rollup_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md24634}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item If a facade is created for a dynamic entry point, this facade will be imported instead of the facaded chunk (\#2575)
\item Manual chunks that include multiple entry points will have proper facades created for all entry points if necessary (\#2575)
\item If missing exports are shimmed, the shim variable will not be global but created on a per-\/module basis and is deconflicted with variables having the same name (\#2584)
\item Missing export shims work properly in System\+JS (\#2584)
\item {\ttfamily preserve\+Modules} now handles dynamic namespace imports (\#2584)
\item Fix chunk execution order in certain scenarios (\#2584)
\item Exports and assignments using destructuring syntax will properly update the exported variables when generating System\+JS output (\#2587)
\item Hashes in chunk names will now also take dynamic imports into account (\#2596)
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_node__modules_2rollup_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md24635}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Pull Requests}{Pull Requests}}\label{md_node__modules_2rollup_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md24635}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \href{https://github.com/rollup/rollup/pull/2565}{\texttt{ \#2565}}\+: Provide module graph information on the plugin context (@samccone)
\item \href{https://github.com/rollup/rollup/pull/2575}{\texttt{ \#2575}}\+: Extend bundle information, tree-\/shake dynamic imports, fix dynamic import facade creation, support manual chunks with multiple entry points, make {\ttfamily optimize\+Chunks} experimental (@lukastaegert)
\item \href{https://github.com/rollup/rollup/pull/2577}{\texttt{ \#2577}}\+: Update dependencies (@lukastaegert)
\item \href{https://github.com/rollup/rollup/pull/2584}{\texttt{ \#2584}}\+: Prune tree-\/shaken chunk imports, fix missing export shimming, support dynamic namespaces when preserving modules, improve chunk execution order (@lukastaegert)
\item \href{https://github.com/rollup/rollup/pull/2587}{\texttt{ \#2587}}\+: Support exports using destructuring declarations and assignments in System\+JS (@lukastaegert)
\item \href{https://github.com/rollup/rollup/pull/2590}{\texttt{ \#2590}}\+: Make sure chunk ids do not contain invalid characters to allow for chunks to correspond to virtual modules (@lukastaegert)
\item \href{https://github.com/rollup/rollup/pull/2594}{\texttt{ \#2594}}\+: Simplify UMD wrapper code and make sure it works in strict mode (@lukastaegert)
\item \href{https://github.com/rollup/rollup/pull/2596}{\texttt{ \#2596}}\+: Take both static and dynamic dependencies into account when calculating hashes (@lukastaegert)
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_node__modules_2rollup_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md24636}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{0.\+67.\+4}{0.67.4}}\label{md_node__modules_2rollup_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md24636}
{\itshape 2018-\/12-\/03}\hypertarget{md_node__modules_2rollup_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md24637}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Bug Fixes}{Bug Fixes}}\label{md_node__modules_2rollup_2CHANGELOG_autotoc_md24637}

\item {\ttfamily options.\+resolve\+Id}, {\ttfamily options.\+resolve\+External} and {\ttfamily options.\+load} can each be a function or an array of functions. If an array, the first non-\/null/undefined return value is used. In both cases, failed resolution/loading will fall back to the defaults, unless an error is thrown. (\href{https://github.com/rollup/rollup/pull/174}{\texttt{ \#174}})

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item BREAKING -\/ {\ttfamily resolve\+Path} is now {\ttfamily resolve\+Id}. The returned {\ttfamily id} (which by default is a filepath) is passed to the {\ttfamily load} function, which can optionally be overridden, and which is applied to all modules including the entry module. This allows custom resolver and loading logic for integration with third party systems (e.\+g. JSPM) or, eventually, in-\/browser usage (\href{https://github.com/rollup/rollup/issues/30}{\texttt{ \#30}})
\item A statement cannot appear after later statements from the same bundle (\href{https://github.com/rollup/rollup/issues/34}{\texttt{ \#34}})
